103|dd2193|

106|e1e6f6|                    for (i, word) in words.enumerated() {
107|68dd69|                        let chunk = (i == 0 ? "" : " ") + word
108|811729|                        continuation.yield(String(chunk))
109|5dcda0|                        try await Task.sleep(nanoseconds: 10_000_000) // 10ms
110|c9717a|                    }
111|dd2193|

127|e66206|    /// Updates suggestions based on the current text and cursor.

131|6224c3|    func updateSuggestions(for text: String, cursorPosition: Int) {
132|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
133|97fb6b|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else {

135|bef5d6|            return

137|adc83b|
138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()
139|042f0f|        guard !prefixLower.isEmpty else {
140|bacf86|            // If user just typed a dot, show members even with empty prefix.

231|f6601a|    private func completionContext(in text: String, cursorPosition: Int) -> CompletionContext? {
232|4c2df9|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return nil }
233|d6ed84|        
234|42915b|        // Safety check: ensure cursorPosition is within bounds
235|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
236|1fae78|        let cursorIndex = text.index(text.startIndex, offsetBy: safeCursor)
237|adc83b|
238|5aebf3|        // Find start of current identifier (letters/digits/_).
239|39f169|        var start = cursorIndex
240|26ebb3|        while start > text.startIndex {
241|c5c76e|            let prev = text.index(before: start)
242|9f8a31|            if isIdentifierChar(text[prev]) {
243|1929f8|                start = prev
244|f5a6eb|            } else {
245|74cfd8|                break
246|a7dc16|            }
247|5f3077|        }
248|adc83b|
249|bf292f|        let prefix = String(text[start..<cursorIndex])
250|adc83b|
251|824562|        // Member completion if immediately preceded by '.'
252|e374b4|        var isMember = false
253|e47c72|        var memberBase: String? = nil
254|adc83b|
255|0c2c38|        if start > text.startIndex {
256|2aa058|            let dotIndex = text.index(before: start)
257|88bd65|            if text[dotIndex] == "." {
258|ca8397|                isMember = true
259|adc83b|
260|6f6689|                // Parse identifier before '.'
261|91f615|                var baseEnd = dotIndex
262|521a36|                var baseStart = baseEnd
263|5fa357|                while baseStart > text.startIndex {
264|56e352|                    let prev = text.index(before: baseStart)
265|2a8ddd|                    if isIdentifierChar(text[prev]) {
266|fbabfa|                        baseStart = prev
267|540066|                    } else {
268|28a64b|                        break
269|c9717a|                    }
270|4e2d32|                }
271|f96abf|                let base = String(text[baseStart..<baseEnd])
272|ce472b|                if !base.isEmpty {
273|b9c992|                    memberBase = base
274|4e2d32|                }
275|a7dc16|            }
276|5f3077|        }
277|adc83b|
278|081616|        return CompletionContext(prefix: prefix,
279|c93ac4|                                 replacementRange: start..<cursorIndex,
280|a50c25|                                 isMemberCompletion: isMember,
281|ee9636|                                 memberBase: memberBase)
282|27e597|    }
283|adc83b|
284|818e4b|    private func isIdentifierChar(_ c: Character) -> Bool {
285|c233b9|        // Swift identifiers are more complex, but this is enough for basic autocomplete.
286|a164d4|        return c.isLetter || c.isNumber || c == "_"
287|27e597|    }

289|117bcf|    private func memberCandidates(forBase base: String) -> [String] {
290|cf1cb2|        // Basic heuristic: only match known stdlib types by exact name.
291|622249|        if let members = memberCompletions[base] { return members }
292|b72a10|        return []
293|27e597|    }
294|adc83b|
295|6ba6d8|    private func extractSymbols(from text: String) -> [String] {
296|1098cf|        // Very lightweight symbol extraction: looks for common declarations.
297|141450|        // Intentionally best-effort; keeps FEAT-046 self-contained.
298|f746d2|        var results = Set<String>()
299|adc83b|
300|f97d0d|        func addMatches(pattern: String) {
301|ca0afa|            guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []) else { return }
302|6c811f|            let ns = text as NSString
303|b25f5b|            let range = NSRange(location: 0, length: ns.length)
304|d25847|            regex.enumerateMatches(in: text, options: [], range: range) { match, _, _ in
305|14f5aa|                guard let match, match.numberOfRanges >= 2 else { return }
306|345d9a|                let nameRange = match.range(at: 1)
307|de56e8|                guard nameRange.location != NSNotFound else { return }
308|8989a1|                let name = ns.substring(with: nameRange)
309|66b469|                if !name.isEmpty { results.insert(name) }
310|a7dc16|            }
311|5f3077|        }
312|adc83b|
313|a1c515|        // func Foo
314|cd4071|        addMatches(pattern: "\\bfunc\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
315|5eaefb|        // class/struct/enum/protocol/typealias Foo
316|685691|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:class|struct|enum|protocol|typealias)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
317|3764b8|        // let/var foo (captures first name before : = , )
318|bbf05c|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:let|var)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)(?=\\s*[:=,])")
319|adc83b|
320|01a90c|        return results.sorted { $0.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare($1) == .orderedAscending }
321|27e597|    }
322|adc83b|
323|1470f2|    private func mergeAndSort(_ items: [Suggestion]) -> [Suggestion] {
324|ff1146|        // Keep highest-scored entry per id.
325|f6e288|        var bestById: [String: Suggestion] = [:]
326|686171|        for item in items {
327|0701eb|            if let existing = bestById[item.id] {
328|d5a6de|                if item.score > existing.score {
329|763640|                    bestById[item.id] = item
330|4e2d32|                }
331|f5a6eb|            } else {
332|b949a2|                bestById[item.id] = item
333|a7dc16|            }
334|5f3077|        }
335|adc83b|
336|cfe5f9|        return bestById.values.sorted {
337|708c2d|            if $0.score != $1.score { return $0.score > $1.score }
338|e5aa71|            return $0.displayText.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare($1.displayText) == .orderedAscending
339|5f3077|        }
340|27e597|    }
341|adc83b|
342|ba218c|    private func apply(items: [Suggestion]) {

345|c77b90|        showSuggestions = !items.isEmpty
346|81a6a8|        selectedIndex = 0

118|d4d7a7|                self.lruOrder.append(key)
119|a7dc16|            }
120|5f3077|        }
121|27e597|    }
122|b4687f|    
123|06e36f|    /// Clears all entries from the cache.
124|5416f6|    func clear() {
125|2eb06b|        cacheQueue.async(flags: .barrier) { [weak self] in
126|1e7e79|            self?.cache.removeAll()
127|a434d2|            self?.lruOrder.removeAll()
128|5f3077|        }
129|27e597|    }

132|b4687f|    
133|e268ba|    /// Removes a key from the LRU order tracking
134|9850b8|    private func removeFromLRU(_ key: String) {
135|acf9f5|        lruOrder.removeAll { $0 == key }
136|27e597|    }
137|b4687f|    
138|4e5908|    /// Updates LRU order by moving the accessed key to the end (most recently used)
139|e5b0f9|    private func updateLRUOrder(_ key: String) {
140|33983e|        removeFromLRU(key)
141|b3c36a|        lruOrder.append(key)
142|27e597|    }

145|9bba21|    private func evictLRUEntry() {
146|1374a3|        guard !lruOrder.isEmpty else { return }
147|d6ed84|

150|27e597|    }

162|8d693c|                removeFromLRU(key)
163|a7dc16|            }

2|421767|import Combine
3|adc83b|
4|910fc8|/// Manages inline code suggestions with debouncing, throttling, and cancellation support.
5|a3a85a|/// Uses Combine operators to prevent excessive API calls while maintaining responsive UX.
6|e0ad8a|/// 
7|eafd18|/// Request Flow:
8|59449b|/// 1. User types → typingSubject receives event
9|4129a0|/// 2. Cancel any pending request immediately (prevent stale results)

176|144775|    @discardableResult
177|d82f01|    func partialAccept() -> String? {
178|cc51cf|        guard let suggestion = currentSuggestion else {
179|1c8557|            return nil
180|5f3077|        }
181|d6ed84|        
182|35c2c0|        // Check if we've already fully accepted the suggestion

196|d6ed84|

199|d6ed84|

226|886d26|    /// Sets up the Combine pipeline with debounce and throttle operators.
227|7cfeb1|    /// 
228|2302ea|    /// Pipeline flow:
229|fcd00b|    /// 1. typingSubject receives events
230|a7ce76|    /// 2. debounce(0.3s): Wait 300ms after user stops typing
231|a5971a|    /// 3. throttle(2.0s): Max 1 event per 2 seconds (latest=true for responsive updates)
232|c17292|    /// 4. removeDuplicates: Filter identical events
233|627455|    /// 5. filter: Remove empty/unworthy contexts
234|6f85e6|    /// 6. flatMap: Execute async fetch with cancellation support
235|2181d5|    private func setupSuggestionPipeline() {
236|ca13c2|        pipelineCancellable = typingSubject
237|0245e4|            // STEP 1: DEBOUNCE (300ms)
238|70cff9|            // Wait 300ms after user stops typing before processing
239|d9fce5|            // This prevents firing requests while user is actively typing
240|84dd17|            .debounce(for: .seconds(debounceInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main)
241|3070d1|            
242|89fc5a|            // STEP 2: THROTTLE (2 seconds)
243|dbb01b|            // Maximum 1 request per 2 seconds
244|bce2c6|            // latest=true ensures we get the most recent event if multiple occur within throttle window
245|ecc467|            .throttle(for: .seconds(throttleInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main, latest: true)
246|3070d1|            
247|844254|            // STEP 3: REMOVE DUPLICATES
248|413909|            // Filter out events with identical content and position
249|0a99da|            // This prevents duplicate API calls for the same context
250|cf49b3|            .removeDuplicates()
251|3070d1|            
252|202ed6|            // STEP 4: FILTER WORTHY CONTEXTS
253|a23af6|            // Only proceed if we have meaningful content to get suggestions for
254|845b1e|            .filter { [weak self] event in
255|06905f|                guard let self = self else { return false }
256|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
257|cc659b|                return self.shouldRequestSuggestion(context: context)
258|a7dc16|            }
259|3070d1|            
260|339920|            // STEP 5: FLATMAP TO ASYNC FETCH
261|2bc815|            // Transform each event into a publisher that fetches suggestions
262|dbc22b|            // This creates a new async context that can be cancelled
263|11fcbf|            .flatMap { [weak self] event -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> in
264|ec615d|                guard let self = self else {
265|6156c3|                    return Just(nil).eraseToAnyPublisher()
266|4e2d32|                }
267|216278|                
268|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
269|6830af|                return self.createFetchPublisher(for: context)
270|a7dc16|            }
271|4de6c5|            // Ensure we receive on main thread for UI updates
272|a8597a|            .receive(on: DispatchQueue.main)
273|1051e2|            .sink { [weak self] suggestion in
274|518c9e|                self?.currentSuggestion = suggestion
275|02c979|                self?.isLoading = false
276|a7dc16|            }
277|27e597|    }
278|b4687f|    
279|984754|    /// Creates a Combine publisher that performs the async suggestion fetch.
280|f2b66e|    /// This allows the fetch to be cancelled when new events arrive.
281|4c0331|    private func createFetchPublisher(for context: SuggestionContext) -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> {
282|c401a0|        // Cancel any existing fetch task
283|f12123|        fetchTask?.cancel()
284|d6ed84|        
285|1c5d21|        // Create new async task for fetching
286|6b1f07|        let task = Task { [weak self] () -> String? in
287|8c11f0|            guard let self = self else { return nil }
288|3070d1|            
289|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
290|7494b5|                self.isLoading = true
291|db594a|                self.lastError = nil
292|a7dc16|            }
293|3070d1|            
294|71cc09|            do {
295|88792d|                // Perform the actual fetch
296|5f8cb1|                let suggestion = try await self.fetchSuggestion(for: context)
297|216278|                
298|056141|                // Check if cancelled before updating UI
299|ac578d|                try Task.checkCancellation()
300|d0b7e3|                return suggestion
301|57e5c6|            } catch is CancellationError {
302|9f1433|                // Task was cancelled - return nil silently
303|15034a|                return nil
304|91b9a2|            } catch {
305|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
306|98968a|                    self.lastError = error
307|4e2d32|                }
308|15034a|                return nil
309|a7dc16|            }
310|5f3077|        }
311|d6ed84|        
312|5854c9|        fetchTask = task
313|d6ed84|        
314|544041|        // Convert the async task to a publisher
315|5c40d7|        return Future<String?, Never> { promise in
316|47ed67|            Task {
317|458ee4|                let result = await task.value
318|67db9f|                promise(.success(result))
319|a7dc16|            }
320|5f3077|        }
321|3dc442|        .eraseToAnyPublisher()
322|27e597|    }

92|a9ed45|                do {

106|e1e6f6|                    for (i, word) in words.enumerated() {
107|68dd69|                        let chunk = (i == 0 ? "" : " ") + word
108|811729|                        continuation.yield(String(chunk))
109|5dcda0|                        try await Task.sleep(nanoseconds: 10_000_000) // 10ms
110|c9717a|                    }
111|dd2193|

114|39aec1|                    continuation.finish(throwing: error)

116|a7dc16|            }
117|5f3077|        }
118|27e597|    }

192|e53e63|    private func buildPrompt(messages: [(role: String, content: String)], systemPrompt: String?) -> String {
193|932a29|        // Nanbeige4.1 uses a specific chat template
194|6c4a5a|        var prompt = ""
195|d6ed84|        
196|d6b133|        // System prompt
197|c7b56e|        let system = systemPrompt ?? "You are a helpful coding assistant running locally on iPad. You are Nanbeige4.1-3B, a compact but powerful language model. Help with code, explain concepts, and assist with development tasks. Be concise and accurate."

199|d6ed84|

202|3ef023|            prompt += "\(msg.role)\n\(msg.content)\n"
203|5f3077|        }
204|d6ed84|        
205|e668ce|        // Prompt for assistant response
206|0a0019|        prompt += "assistant\n"
207|d6ed84|        
208|dd02e7|        return prompt
209|27e597|    }

91|fb529e|    static func parse(_ text: String) -> (cleanText: String, attributes: [NSRange: [NSAttributedString.Key: Any]]) {
92|567730|        var cleanText = ""
93|6dcfe0|        var attributes: [NSRange: [NSAttributedString.Key: Any]] = [:]
94|3029d6|        var currentIndex = 0
95|d6ed84|        
96|a155f2|        var currentForeground: Color?

99|ed4605|        var isItalic = false
100|04e5cf|        var isUnderline = false
101|d6ed84|        
102|18bc61|        // Pattern to match ANSI escape sequences
103|2fcf29|        let pattern = "\u{001B}\\[([0-9;]*)m"
104|a4a259|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []) else {
105|49526f|            return (text, [:])
106|5f3077|        }
107|d6ed84|        
108|8f9408|        let nsRange = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
109|a1371b|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, options: [], range: nsRange)
110|d6ed84|        
111|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
112|d6ed84|        
113|847e6d|        for match in matches {
114|4f4bc8|            let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text)!
115|0e558e|            let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text)!
116|6e244b|            let codes = text[codeRange].split(separator: ";").compactMap { Int($0) }
117|3070d1|            
118|c4f420|            // Append text before the escape code
119|81b001|            let textBefore = String(text[lastEnd..<matchRange.lowerBound])
120|b8d035|            if !textBefore.isEmpty {
121|16a34c|                let nsRange = NSRange(location: currentIndex, length: textBefore.utf16.count)
122|216278|                
123|463445|                var attrs: [NSAttributedString.Key: Any] = [:]
124|e6835d|                if let fg = currentForeground {
125|073262|                    attrs[.foregroundColor] = fg
126|4e2d32|                }
127|8019e1|                if let bg = currentBackground {
128|9ade39|                    attrs[.backgroundColor] = bg
129|4e2d32|                }
130|7da01b|                if isBold {
131|0ccd26|                    attrs[.font] = Font.system(.body, design: .monospaced).bold()
132|4e2d32|                }
133|06eada|                if isItalic {
134|31a08a|                    attrs[.font] = Font.system(.body, design: .monospaced).italic()
135|4e2d32|                }
136|bddabc|                if isUnderline {
137|350264|                    attrs[.underlineStyle] = NSUnderlineStyle.single.rawValue
138|4e2d32|                }
139|216278|                
140|17bc14|                if !attrs.isEmpty {
141|1596df|                    attributes[nsRange] = attrs
142|4e2d32|                }
143|216278|                
144|f5048d|                cleanText.append(textBefore)
145|cfcda0|                currentIndex += textBefore.utf16.count
146|a7dc16|            }
147|3070d1|            
148|4099c7|            // Process SGR codes
149|e5fe4b|            if codes.isEmpty || codes.contains(0) {
150|264ba9|                // Reset
151|526e69|                currentForeground = nil
152|a963ce|                currentBackground = nil
153|945610|                isBold = false
154|80d4db|                isItalic = false

156|f5a6eb|            } else {
157|3ed108|                for code in codes {
158|2d0579|                    switch code {
159|cd8b61|                    case 1: isBold = true
160|20ad36|                    case 3: isItalic = true
161|4d8e2e|                    case 4: isUnderline = true
162|dba504|                    case 22: isBold = false
163|edbca4|                    case 23: isItalic = false
164|09f664|                    case 24: isUnderline = false
165|b00b80|                    case 30...37, 90...97:
166|7057ef|                        currentForeground = foregroundColors[code]
167|b55fb7|                    case 40...47, 100...107:
168|0d0d47|                        currentBackground = backgroundColors[code]
169|853318|                    default:
170|28a64b|                        break
171|c9717a|                    }
172|4e2d32|                }
173|a7dc16|            }
174|3070d1|            
175|3e274c|            lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
176|5f3077|        }
177|d6ed84|        
178|5fc192|        // Append remaining text
179|817921|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...])
180|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
181|ecd40c|            let nsRange = NSRange(location: currentIndex, length: remainingText.utf16.count)
182|3070d1|            
183|e08fe8|            var attrs: [NSAttributedString.Key: Any] = [:]
184|52845f|            if let fg = currentForeground {
185|91e89f|                attrs[.foregroundColor] = fg
186|a7dc16|            }
187|06f74f|            if let bg = currentBackground {
188|6f8da0|                attrs[.backgroundColor] = bg
189|a7dc16|            }
190|a7db39|            if isBold {
191|fd229d|                attrs[.font] = Font.system(.body, design: .monospaced).bold()
192|a7dc16|            }
193|305097|            if isItalic {
194|bdba36|                attrs[.font] = Font.system(.body, design: .monospaced).italic()
195|a7dc16|            }
196|97543a|            if isUnderline {
197|5e6d92|                attrs[.underlineStyle] = NSUnderlineStyle.single.rawValue
198|a7dc16|            }
199|3070d1|            
200|6c040a|            if !attrs.isEmpty {
201|8370c6|                attributes[nsRange] = attrs
202|a7dc16|            }
203|3070d1|

205|5f3077|        }
206|d6ed84|        
207|c7093f|        return (cleanText, attributes)
208|27e597|    }

103|dd2193|                    
104|e9720e|                    // Simulate streaming by yielding chunks
105|8def0a|                    let words = response.split(separator: " ")
106|e1e6f6|                    for (i, word) in words.enumerated() {
107|68dd69|                        let chunk = (i == 0 ? "" : " ") + word
108|811729|                        continuation.yield(String(chunk))
109|5dcda0|                        try await Task.sleep(nanoseconds: 10_000_000) // 10ms
110|c9717a|                    }
111|dd2193|                    
112|c65a9a|                    continuation.finish()
113|6bf1ca|                } catch {
114|39aec1|                    continuation.finish(throwing: error)
115|4e2d32|                }
116|a7dc16|            }
117|5f3077|        }

952|cdbd69|You are an expert coding assistant integrated into a code editor on iPadOS. You help developers write, debug, explain, and improve their code.
953|adc83b|
954|3584f0|Guidelines:
955|9e10fd|- Provide clear, concise explanations
956|d9814a|- Use code blocks with proper language tags for code snippets
957|fab31f|- Suggest best practices and optimizations
958|17f65d|- Be helpful with debugging and error resolution
959|a2707f|- When generating code, ensure it's complete and runnable
960|e4615a|"""
961|d6ed84|

963|b91f6a|            prompt += "\n\nCurrent file context:\n```\n\(context)\n```"

968|b4687f|    
969|c53a51|    private func extractCodeBlocks(from text: String) -> [CodeBlock] {
970|791eb5|        var blocks: [CodeBlock] = []
971|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
972|d6ed84|        
973|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
974|f7ed63|            return blocks
975|5f3077|        }
976|d6ed84|        
977|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
978|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
979|d6ed84|        
980|847e6d|        for match in matches {
981|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
982|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
983|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
984|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
985|9e5c94|                blocks.append(CodeBlock(language: language.isEmpty ? "text" : language, code: code))
986|a7dc16|            }
987|5f3077|        }
988|d6ed84|        
989|db7106|        return blocks
990|27e597|    }

178|4c2551|    func runFile(path: String, via sshManager: SSHManager) async throws {
179|ee913b|        guard sshManager.isConnected else {
180|a2276b|            throw SSHClientError.notConnected
181|5f3077|        }
182|d6ed84|        
183|25e543|        let language = detectLanguage(from: path)
184|1c1bfd|        let interpreter = RemoteSupportedLanguage(rawValue: language)?.interpreter ?? language
185|d6ed84|        
186|2c2d95|        // Build command based on language
187|49e4a0|        let command: String

189|1c8542|        case "swift":
190|ed2b09|            command = "swift \(path)"
191|bbd027|        case "python", "python3":
192|8e3fde|            command = "python3 \(path)"
193|0db04c|        case "node":
194|86436d|            command = "node \(path)"
195|ee50e6|        case "go":
196|19cee7|            command = "cd $(dirname \(path)) && go run $(basename \(path))"
197|ced789|        case "rust":
198|2cb8e5|            let binaryName = (path as NSString).lastPathComponent.replacingOccurrences(of: ".rs", with: "")

200|8cc904|        case "cpp":
201|750f8c|            let binaryName = UUID().uuidString
202|2d3c9c|            command = "g++ \(path) -o /tmp/\(binaryName) && /tmp/\(binaryName)"
203|79273a|        case "c":
204|750f8c|            let binaryName = UUID().uuidString
205|3702e2|            command = "gcc \(path) -o /tmp/\(binaryName) && /tmp/\(binaryName)"
206|520b7d|        default:
207|c4ac4a|            command = "\(interpreter) \(path)"
208|5f3077|        }

210|df86d1|        try await runCommand(command: command, via: sshManager)
211|27e597|    }

213|e40fb0|    /// Run a command on the remote server
214|3aab3f|    func runCommand(command: String, via sshManager: SSHManager) async throws {
215|ee913b|        guard sshManager.isConnected else {
216|a2276b|            throw SSHClientError.notConnected
217|5f3077|        }
218|d6ed84|        
219|ee83d4|        // Reset state
220|8e25b2|        await resetState()
221|d6ed84|        
222|800dd1|        // Create process record
223|3bef75|        let process = RemoteProcess(
224|87869c|            command: command,
225|e7cc59|            pid: nil,
226|247345|            startTime: Date(),
227|739210|            exitCode: nil,
228|d7d37d|            endTime: nil
229|3143a4|        )
230|d6ed84|        
231|84c5ec|        await MainActor.run {
232|0b4ee8|            self.currentProcess = process
233|e27aa5|            self.isRunning = true
234|5f3077|        }
235|d6ed84|        
236|e436df|        // Build command with working directory if specified
237|7c267c|        let finalCommand: String
238|227cae|        if let cwd = workingDirectory {
239|af9d9d|            finalCommand = "cd '\(cwd)' && \(command)"
240|b31999|        } else {
241|507adb|            finalCommand = command
242|5f3077|        }
243|d6ed84|        
244|8a77a6|        // Execute via SSH with streaming
245|541668|        let stream = executeCommandStreaming(
246|dc4dd5|            command: finalCommand,
247|5bbfaa|            environment: environmentVariables,
248|de011a|            timeout: defaultTimeout,
249|669695|            via: sshManager
250|3143a4|        )
251|d6ed84|        
252|b84546|        // Process the stream
253|2e192c|        var outputBuffer = ""
254|0deb8f|        var receivedExit = false
255|d6ed84|        
256|4da690|        do {
257|0547b1|            for try await outputEvent in stream {
258|5b1a5e|                switch outputEvent {
259|f151c9|                case .stdout(let text):
260|a56a22|                    outputBuffer.append(text)
261|72e736|                    await MainActor.run {
262|2f7b4c|                        self.output.append(text)
263|c9717a|                    }
264|dd2193|                    
265|cabb36|                case .stderr(let text):
266|a73586|                    outputBuffer.append("[stderr] \(text)")
267|72e736|                    await MainActor.run {
268|0bf02e|                        self.output.append("[stderr] \(text)")
269|c9717a|                    }
270|dd2193|                    
271|f2d98c|                case .exit(let code):
272|4f3ed8|                    receivedExit = true
273|72e736|                    await MainActor.run {
274|6d4aec|                        self.lastExitCode = Int(code)
275|0024c2|                        if var process = self.currentProcess {
276|67c3e1|                            process.exitCode = Int(code)
277|0e26a0|                            process.endTime = Date()
278|f33135|                            self.currentProcess = process
279|65a061|                            self.processHistory.append(process)
280|392b35|                        }
281|c0305c|                        self.isRunning = false
282|c9717a|                    }
283|dd2193|                    
284|b50a83|                case .timeout:
285|19b19d|                    outputBuffer.append("\n[Command timed out after \(defaultTimeout) seconds]")
286|72e736|                    await MainActor.run {
287|78732a|                        self.output.append("\n[Command timed out after \(self.defaultTimeout) seconds]")
288|c0305c|                        self.isRunning = false
289|332dee|                        self.lastExitCode = -1
290|c9717a|                    }
291|dd2193|                    
292|0e578a|                case .error(let error):
293|a7f8db|                    throw error
294|4e2d32|                }
295|a7dc16|            }
296|3070d1|            
297|bd011c|            // If no exit code was received, mark as completed
298|5ad710|            if !receivedExit {
299|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
300|d34780|                    self.isRunning = false
301|28cc9a|                    if var process = self.currentProcess {
302|5ba53b|                        process.exitCode = self.lastExitCode ?? 0
303|33f76d|                        process.endTime = Date()
304|00b506|                        self.currentProcess = process
305|ab0475|                        self.processHistory.append(process)
306|c9717a|                    }
307|4e2d32|                }
308|a7dc16|            }
309|3070d1|            
310|853889|        } catch {
311|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
312|f029ce|                self.isRunning = false
313|5723f1|                self.output.append("\n[Error: \(error.localizedDescription)]")
314|a7dc16|            }
315|864dfa|            throw error
316|5f3077|        }
317|27e597|    }

319|bd227b|    /// Run a code selection on the remote server
320|9e91d6|    func runSelection(code: String, language: String, via sshManager: SSHManager) async throws {
321|ee913b|        guard sshManager.isConnected else {
322|a2276b|            throw SSHClientError.notConnected
323|5f3077|        }
324|d6ed84|

326|2f2c6c|        let tempFileName = "vscode_ipad_\(UUID().uuidString)\(fileExtension(for: language))"
327|a10ef3|        let tempPath = "/tmp/\(tempFileName)"
328|d6ed84|        
329|671dbc|        // Escape the code for shell

333|81c43c|            .replacingOccurrences(of: "\n", with: "\\n")
334|d6ed84|

336|1c1bfd|        let interpreter = RemoteSupportedLanguage(rawValue: language)?.interpreter ?? language
337|90cb1c|        let runCommand: String

345|3070d1|            
346|bbd027|        case "python", "python3":

349|bd2938|            runCommand = "\(createFileCmd) && \(runCmd) && rm \(tempPath)"
350|3070d1|

352|2463f3|            let createFileCmd = "printf '%b' '\(escapedCode)' > \(tempPath)"
353|0f6b2e|            let runCmd = "node \(tempPath)"
354|bd2938|            runCommand = "\(createFileCmd) && \(runCmd) && rm \(tempPath)"
355|3070d1|            
356|9f8131|        case "bash", "sh":
357|feb049|            // For bash, we can use heredoc or direct execution
358|ef4846|            runCommand = "bash -c '\(escapedCode)'"
359|3070d1|            
360|f6a68d|        case "ruby":
361|2463f3|            let createFileCmd = "printf '%b' '\(escapedCode)' > \(tempPath)"
362|5a2cd2|            let runCmd = "ruby \(tempPath)"
363|bd2938|            runCommand = "\(createFileCmd) && \(runCmd) && rm \(tempPath)"
364|3070d1|            
365|520b7d|        default:
366|2463f3|            let createFileCmd = "printf '%b' '\(escapedCode)' > \(tempPath)"

368|bd2938|            runCommand = "\(createFileCmd) && \(runCmd) && rm \(tempPath)"

372|27e597|    }

423|cb7007|    /// Kill the current running process
424|8a737e|    func kill() {
425|242f84|        // Close the active channel if any
426|6c5325|        if let channel = activeChannel {
427|f1c133|            channel.close(promise: nil)
428|7d1ca7|            activeChannel = nil
429|5f3077|        }
430|d6ed84|        
431|f1a4e8|        // Signal continuation to finish
432|856ef4|        activeContinuation?.finish()
433|e66f0f|        activeContinuation = nil
434|d6ed84|        
435|6422f4|        // Update state
436|e6ae78|        if isRunning {
437|97537f|            output.append("\n[Process terminated by user]")
438|86f671|            isRunning = false
439|3070d1|            
440|37eb79|            if var process = currentProcess {
441|3a267c|                process.exitCode = -9 // SIGKILL
442|bbfcc4|                process.endTime = Date()
443|d89d12|                currentProcess = process
444|69851e|                processHistory.append(process)
445|a7dc16|            }
446|3070d1|            
447|2902e8|            lastExitCode = -9
448|5f3077|        }
449|27e597|    }

195|46f2b0|    func save(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
196|518562|        var config = connection
197|33d6e7|        config.lastUsed = Date()
198|d6ed84|        
199|b12566|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == config.id }) {
200|ca9b5c|            savedConnections[index] = config
201|b31999|        } else {
202|979f69|            savedConnections.append(config)
203|5f3077|        }
204|d6ed84|        
205|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
206|27e597|    }
207|b4687f|    
208|eea006|    func delete(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {

210|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
211|27e597|    }
212|b4687f|    
213|c2f169|    func updateLastUsed(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
214|2e9633|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == connection.id }) {
215|85969b|            savedConnections[index].lastUsed = Date()
216|da901b|            persistConnections()
217|5f3077|        }
218|27e597|    }
219|b4687f|    
220|ae0029|    private func loadConnections() {
221|e4c350|        guard let data = userDefaults.data(forKey: storageKey),
222|f8ff24|              let connections = try? JSONDecoder().decode([SSHConnectionConfig].self, from: data) else {
223|bef5d6|            return
224|5f3077|        }
225|a65f6e|        savedConnections = connections.sorted { ($0.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) > ($1.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) }
226|27e597|    }
227|b4687f|    
228|a3fceb|    private func persistConnections() {
229|7e12a8|        guard let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(savedConnections) else { return }
230|ad5d30|        userDefaults.set(data, forKey: storageKey)
231|27e597|    }

51|d6ed84|

59|d6ed84|

63|150252|                guard let self = self else { return }
64|216278|

67|216278|                
68|4b39b7|                // Remove the prefix for cleaner output display
69|62636a|                var cleanMessage = message

72|11af1f|                        cleanMessage = String(message.dropFirst(prefix.count))
73|28a64b|                        break
74|c9717a|                    }
75|4e2d32|                }
76|216278|

79|5f3077|        }
80|d6ed84|        
81|5a9195|        // Execute the code asynchronously

94|4e2d32|                }

99|216278|

116|7aa5bd|    /// Format a JSValue for display
117|e68bfd|    private func formatJSValue(_ value: JSValue) -> String {
118|c903ed|        if value.isNull {
119|c04d4d|            return "null"
120|35d02e|        } else if value.isUndefined {
121|b32932|            return "undefined"
122|edfa6b|        } else if value.isBoolean {
123|1a76ee|            return value.toBool() ? "true" : "false"
124|4e414f|        } else if value.isNumber {
125|9abc83|            let num = value.toNumber()
126|d3fc6f|            // Check if it's an integer
127|a09f20|            if let n = num, n.doubleValue == Double(n.intValue) {
128|ee9ad8|                return "\(n.intValue)"
129|a7dc16|            }
130|64a140|            return "\(num?.doubleValue ?? 0)"
131|419991|        } else if value.isString {
132|7c8a45|            return "\"\(value.toString() ?? "")\""
133|a72377|        } else if value.isArray {
134|d7f252|            if let array = value.toArray() {
135|c35363|                return "[\(array.map { "\($0)" }.joined(separator: ", "))]"
136|a7dc16|            }
137|976c47|            return "[]"
138|bb3c98|        } else if value.isObject {
139|b4fae0|            if let dict = value.toDictionary() {
140|ee1ab7|                let json = try? JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: dict, options: [.prettyPrinted, .sortedKeys])
141|a9b0f4|                if let json = json, let str = String(data: json, encoding: .utf8) {
142|cfed56|                    return str
143|4e2d32|                }
144|a7dc16|            }
145|0b436d|            return value.toString() ?? "[object]"
146|5f3077|        }
147|bbc620|        return value.toString() ?? "undefined"
148|27e597|    }

196|518562|        var config = connection
197|33d6e7|        config.lastUsed = Date()
198|d6ed84|        
199|b12566|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == config.id }) {
200|ca9b5c|            savedConnections[index] = config
201|b31999|        } else {
202|979f69|            savedConnections.append(config)
203|5f3077|        }
204|d6ed84|        
205|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
206|27e597|    }
207|b4687f|    
208|eea006|    func delete(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {

210|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
211|27e597|    }
212|b4687f|

214|2e9633|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == connection.id }) {
215|85969b|            savedConnections[index].lastUsed = Date()
216|da901b|            persistConnections()
217|5f3077|        }
218|27e597|    }
219|b4687f|    
220|ae0029|    private func loadConnections() {
221|e4c350|        guard let data = userDefaults.data(forKey: storageKey),
222|f8ff24|              let connections = try? JSONDecoder().decode([SSHConnectionConfig].self, from: data) else {
223|bef5d6|            return
224|5f3077|        }
225|a65f6e|        savedConnections = connections.sorted { ($0.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) > ($1.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) }
226|27e597|    }
227|b4687f|    
228|a3fceb|    private func persistConnections() {
229|7e12a8|        guard let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(savedConnections) else { return }
230|ad5d30|        userDefaults.set(data, forKey: storageKey)
231|27e597|    }

182|adc83b|
183|ed830e|class SSHConnectionStore: ObservableObject {
184|98c1cf|    static let shared = SSHConnectionStore()
185|b4687f|    
186|cfe3df|    @Published var savedConnections: [SSHConnectionConfig] = []
187|b4687f|    
188|ee9002|    private let userDefaults = UserDefaults.standard
189|07a977|    private let storageKey = "ssh_saved_connections"
190|b4687f|    
191|359b1b|    init() {
192|a04ada|        loadConnections()
193|27e597|    }
194|b4687f|    
195|46f2b0|    func save(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
196|518562|        var config = connection
197|33d6e7|        config.lastUsed = Date()
198|d6ed84|        
199|b12566|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == config.id }) {
200|ca9b5c|            savedConnections[index] = config
201|b31999|        } else {
202|979f69|            savedConnections.append(config)
203|5f3077|        }
204|d6ed84|        
205|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
206|27e597|    }
207|b4687f|    
208|eea006|    func delete(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
209|015edf|        savedConnections.removeAll { $0.id == connection.id }
210|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
211|27e597|    }
212|b4687f|    
213|c2f169|    func updateLastUsed(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
214|2e9633|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == connection.id }) {
215|85969b|            savedConnections[index].lastUsed = Date()
216|da901b|            persistConnections()
217|5f3077|        }
218|27e597|    }
219|b4687f|    
220|ae0029|    private func loadConnections() {
221|e4c350|        guard let data = userDefaults.data(forKey: storageKey),
222|f8ff24|              let connections = try? JSONDecoder().decode([SSHConnectionConfig].self, from: data) else {
223|bef5d6|            return
224|5f3077|        }
225|a65f6e|        savedConnections = connections.sorted { ($0.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) > ($1.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) }
226|27e597|    }
227|b4687f|    
228|a3fceb|    private func persistConnections() {
229|7e12a8|        guard let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(savedConnections) else { return }
230|ad5d30|        userDefaults.set(data, forKey: storageKey)
231|27e597|    }

47|62811f|    /// - Parameter context: The code context to hash
48|d02457|    /// - Returns: A hex-encoded SHA256 hash string
49|233ae6|    private func hashContext(_ context: String) -> String {
50|ab8594|        let data = Data(context.utf8)
51|97a5e1|        var hash = [UInt8](repeating: 0, count: Int(CC_SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH))
52|3e64b0|        _ = data.withUnsafeBytes { bytes in
53|3e6f69|            CC_SHA256(bytes.baseAddress, CC_LONG(data.count), &hash)
54|5f3077|        }
55|f6441a|        return hash.map { String(format: "%02hhx", $0) }.joined()
56|27e597|    }
57|b4687f|    
58|36e755|    // MARK: - Public API
59|b4687f|    
60|033bf4|    /// Retrieves a cached suggestion for the given code context if it exists and hasn't expired.
61|c435d3|    /// Updates LRU order on successful retrieval.
62|112b9c|    /// - Parameter context: The code context string to look up
63|6d9dea|    /// - Returns: The cached suggestion string, or nil if not found or expired
64|5ba297|    func get(context: String) -> String? {
65|a9c444|        let key = hashContext(context)
66|d6ed84|        
67|98f033|        return cacheQueue.sync {
68|9d266a|            guard let entry = cache[key] else {
69|15034a|                return nil
70|a7dc16|            }
71|3070d1|            
72|2f14e2|            // Check if entry has expired
73|e16ac4|            if entry.isExpired {

75|185e7a|                cache.removeValue(forKey: key)
76|8d693c|                removeFromLRU(key)

79|3070d1|

81|960881|            updateLRUOrder(key)

91|0e56d7|    ///   - suggestion: The AI suggestion to cache
92|682096|    func set(context: String, suggestion: String) {

94|d6ed84|        
95|2eb06b|        cacheQueue.async(flags: .barrier) { [weak self] in
96|2baf81|            guard let self = self else { return }
97|3070d1|

103|43d041|            )

109|664568|                self.updateLRUOrder(key)
110|f5a6eb|            } else {

120|5f3077|        }

226|886d26|    /// Sets up the Combine pipeline with debounce and throttle operators.
227|7cfeb1|    /// 
228|2302ea|    /// Pipeline flow:
229|fcd00b|    /// 1. typingSubject receives events
230|a7ce76|    /// 2. debounce(0.3s): Wait 300ms after user stops typing
231|a5971a|    /// 3. throttle(2.0s): Max 1 event per 2 seconds (latest=true for responsive updates)
232|c17292|    /// 4. removeDuplicates: Filter identical events
233|627455|    /// 5. filter: Remove empty/unworthy contexts
234|6f85e6|    /// 6. flatMap: Execute async fetch with cancellation support
235|2181d5|    private func setupSuggestionPipeline() {
236|ca13c2|        pipelineCancellable = typingSubject
237|0245e4|            // STEP 1: DEBOUNCE (300ms)
238|70cff9|            // Wait 300ms after user stops typing before processing
239|d9fce5|            // This prevents firing requests while user is actively typing
240|84dd17|            .debounce(for: .seconds(debounceInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main)
241|3070d1|            
242|89fc5a|            // STEP 2: THROTTLE (2 seconds)
243|dbb01b|            // Maximum 1 request per 2 seconds
244|bce2c6|            // latest=true ensures we get the most recent event if multiple occur within throttle window
245|ecc467|            .throttle(for: .seconds(throttleInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main, latest: true)
246|3070d1|            
247|844254|            // STEP 3: REMOVE DUPLICATES
248|413909|            // Filter out events with identical content and position
249|0a99da|            // This prevents duplicate API calls for the same context
250|cf49b3|            .removeDuplicates()
251|3070d1|            
252|202ed6|            // STEP 4: FILTER WORTHY CONTEXTS
253|a23af6|            // Only proceed if we have meaningful content to get suggestions for
254|845b1e|            .filter { [weak self] event in
255|06905f|                guard let self = self else { return false }
256|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
257|cc659b|                return self.shouldRequestSuggestion(context: context)
258|a7dc16|            }
259|3070d1|            
260|339920|            // STEP 5: FLATMAP TO ASYNC FETCH
261|2bc815|            // Transform each event into a publisher that fetches suggestions
262|dbc22b|            // This creates a new async context that can be cancelled
263|11fcbf|            .flatMap { [weak self] event -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> in
264|ec615d|                guard let self = self else {
265|6156c3|                    return Just(nil).eraseToAnyPublisher()
266|4e2d32|                }
267|216278|                
268|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
269|6830af|                return self.createFetchPublisher(for: context)
270|a7dc16|            }
271|4de6c5|            // Ensure we receive on main thread for UI updates
272|a8597a|            .receive(on: DispatchQueue.main)
273|1051e2|            .sink { [weak self] suggestion in
274|518c9e|                self?.currentSuggestion = suggestion
275|02c979|                self?.isLoading = false
276|a7dc16|            }
277|27e597|    }
278|b4687f|    
279|984754|    /// Creates a Combine publisher that performs the async suggestion fetch.
280|f2b66e|    /// This allows the fetch to be cancelled when new events arrive.
281|4c0331|    private func createFetchPublisher(for context: SuggestionContext) -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> {
282|c401a0|        // Cancel any existing fetch task
283|f12123|        fetchTask?.cancel()
284|d6ed84|        
285|1c5d21|        // Create new async task for fetching
286|6b1f07|        let task = Task { [weak self] () -> String? in
287|8c11f0|            guard let self = self else { return nil }
288|3070d1|            
289|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
290|7494b5|                self.isLoading = true
291|db594a|                self.lastError = nil
292|a7dc16|            }
293|3070d1|            
294|71cc09|            do {
295|88792d|                // Perform the actual fetch
296|5f8cb1|                let suggestion = try await self.fetchSuggestion(for: context)
297|216278|                
298|056141|                // Check if cancelled before updating UI
299|ac578d|                try Task.checkCancellation()
300|d0b7e3|                return suggestion
301|57e5c6|            } catch is CancellationError {
302|9f1433|                // Task was cancelled - return nil silently
303|15034a|                return nil
304|91b9a2|            } catch {
305|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
306|98968a|                    self.lastError = error
307|4e2d32|                }
308|15034a|                return nil
309|a7dc16|            }

366|2463f3|            let createFileCmd = "printf '%b' '\(escapedCode)' > \(tempPath)"

369|5f3077|        }

372|27e597|    }

127|e66206|    /// Updates suggestions based on the current text and cursor.
128|2cbc84|    ///
129|d91771|    /// FEAT-046: extracts symbols from `text` and mixes them into the suggestion list.
130|785f23|    /// FEAT-047: adds a curated set of Swift stdlib completions.
131|6224c3|    func updateSuggestions(for text: String, cursorPosition: Int) {
132|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
133|97fb6b|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else {
134|0efe98|            apply(items: [])
135|bef5d6|            return
136|5f3077|        }
137|adc83b|
138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()
139|042f0f|        guard !prefixLower.isEmpty else {
140|bacf86|            // If user just typed a dot, show members even with empty prefix.
141|a46e04|            if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
142|c9f7f8|                let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
143|92798d|                let items = members.map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) }
144|0b887c|                apply(items: items)
145|f5a6eb|            } else {
146|4c73d4|                apply(items: [])
147|a7dc16|            }
148|bef5d6|            return
149|5f3077|        }
150|adc83b|
151|3e8861|        var candidates: [Suggestion] = []
152|adc83b|
153|67a42f|        // FEAT-046: current file symbols
154|f70c93|        let symbols = extractSymbols(from: text)
155|27a302|        candidates.append(contentsOf: symbols
156|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
157|9de4dd|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .symbol, displayText: $0, score: 900) })
158|adc83b|
159|5f2431|        // Keywords
160|1a6e20|        candidates.append(contentsOf: keywords
161|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
162|b40e7e|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .keyword, displayText: $0, score: 800) })
163|adc83b|
164|fcf131|        // FEAT-047: Swift stdlib (top level)
165|d76253|        candidates.append(contentsOf: stdlibTopLevel
166|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
167|3cfc84|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .stdlib, displayText: $0, score: 700) })
168|adc83b|
169|07fafa|        // Member completions (very small heuristic-based set)
170|7f874f|        if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
171|68d0ac|            let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
172|a69811|            candidates.append(contentsOf: members
173|585680|                .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
174|73995e|                .map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) })
175|5f3077|        }
176|adc83b|
177|41630d|        // De-dupe + rank
178|673af4|        let merged = mergeAndSort(candidates)
179|678fc2|        apply(items: merged)
180|27e597|    }
181|adc83b|
182|530c2a|    func selectNext() {
183|1052ec|        guard showSuggestions else { return }
184|3185f4|        if selectedIndex < suggestions.count - 1 {
185|f3e28c|            selectedIndex += 1
186|5f3077|        }
187|27e597|    }
188|adc83b|
189|2b2ba9|    func selectPrevious() {
190|1052ec|        guard showSuggestions else { return }
191|1b2b81|        if selectedIndex > 0 {
192|ee2279|            selectedIndex -= 1
193|5f3077|        }
194|27e597|    }
195|adc83b|

197|55f4f4|        guard showSuggestions, selectedIndex < suggestions.count else { return nil }
198|acf4b6|        return suggestions[selectedIndex]
199|27e597|    }

117|e68bfd|    private func formatJSValue(_ value: JSValue) -> String {
118|c903ed|        if value.isNull {
119|c04d4d|            return "null"
120|35d02e|        } else if value.isUndefined {
121|b32932|            return "undefined"
122|edfa6b|        } else if value.isBoolean {
123|1a76ee|            return value.toBool() ? "true" : "false"
124|4e414f|        } else if value.isNumber {
125|9abc83|            let num = value.toNumber()
126|d3fc6f|            // Check if it's an integer
127|a09f20|            if let n = num, n.doubleValue == Double(n.intValue) {
128|ee9ad8|                return "\(n.intValue)"
129|a7dc16|            }
130|64a140|            return "\(num?.doubleValue ?? 0)"
131|419991|        } else if value.isString {
132|7c8a45|            return "\"\(value.toString() ?? "")\""
133|a72377|        } else if value.isArray {
134|d7f252|            if let array = value.toArray() {
135|c35363|                return "[\(array.map { "\($0)" }.joined(separator: ", "))]"
136|a7dc16|            }
137|976c47|            return "[]"
138|bb3c98|        } else if value.isObject {
139|b4fae0|            if let dict = value.toDictionary() {
140|ee1ab7|                let json = try? JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: dict, options: [.prettyPrinted, .sortedKeys])
141|a9b0f4|                if let json = json, let str = String(data: json, encoding: .utf8) {
142|cfed56|                    return str
143|4e2d32|                }
144|a7dc16|            }
145|0b436d|            return value.toString() ?? "[object]"
146|5f3077|        }
147|bbc620|        return value.toString() ?? "undefined"
148|27e597|    }

257|d326c6|    func connect(config: RemoteDebuggerConfig, sshConfig: SSHConnectionConfig) async throws {
258|0c76b9|        self.config = config
259|58134f|        self.debuggerType = config.debuggerType
260|d6ed84|        
261|5673e6|        state = .connecting
262|bc7fbc|        emitEvent(.stateChanged(.connecting))
263|d6ed84|        
264|0bf4a9|        // Create and configure SSH manager
265|fbb1dc|        let ssh = SSHManager()
266|26c4e6|        self.sshManager = ssh
267|d6ed84|        
268|94f4d1|        // Set up SSH delegate to receive output
269|51d252|        let outputHandler = SSHOutputHandler(debugger: self)
270|831741|        ssh.delegate = outputHandler
271|d6ed84|        
272|813ed1|        // Connect via SSH
273|7ba7c7|        try await withCheckedThrowingContinuation { (continuation: CheckedContinuation<Void, Error>) in
274|af5471|            ssh.connect(config: sshConfig) { result in
275|7a4073|                switch result {
276|2cfe35|                case .success:
277|7115ac|                    continuation.resume()
278|6b00fe|                case .failure(let error):
279|773145|                    continuation.resume(throwing: error)
280|4e2d32|                }
281|a7dc16|            }
282|5f3077|        }
283|d6ed84|        
284|87d109|        state = .connected
285|419741|        emitEvent(.stateChanged(.connected))
286|d6ed84|

288|a3253f|        try await startDebugger()
289|27e597|    }

970|c53a51|    private func extractCodeBlocks(from text: String) -> [CodeBlock] {
971|791eb5|        var blocks: [CodeBlock] = []
972|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
973|d6ed84|        
974|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
975|f7ed63|            return blocks
976|5f3077|        }
977|d6ed84|        
978|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
979|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
980|d6ed84|        
981|847e6d|        for match in matches {
982|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
983|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
984|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
985|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
986|9e5c94|                blocks.append(CodeBlock(language: language.isEmpty ? "text" : language, code: code))
987|a7dc16|            }
988|5f3077|        }
989|d6ed84|        
990|db7106|        return blocks
991|27e597|    }

200|ca9b5c|            savedConnections[index] = config

206|27e597|    }
207|b4687f|

211|27e597|    }

216|da901b|            persistConnections()
217|5f3077|        }
218|27e597|    }

221|e4c350|        guard let data = userDefaults.data(forKey: storageKey),
222|f8ff24|              let connections = try? JSONDecoder().decode([SSHConnectionConfig].self, from: data) else {
223|bef5d6|            return
224|5f3077|        }
225|a65f6e|        savedConnections = connections.sorted { ($0.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) > ($1.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) }
226|27e597|    }
227|b4687f|    
228|a3fceb|    private func persistConnections() {
229|7e12a8|        guard let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(savedConnections) else { return }
230|ad5d30|        userDefaults.set(data, forKey: storageKey)
231|27e597|    }

158|cb81b4|    private func canonicalFileId(_ file: String) -> String {
159|e998da|        // Many call sites use URL.absoluteString; convert file:// URLs to paths so we
160|b513c2|        // don't end up with duplicate breakpoint buckets for the same file.
161|9942cc|        if let url = URL(string: file), url.isFileURL {
162|bdef50|            return url.path
163|5f3077|        }
164|374ff6|        return file
165|27e597|    }
166|adc83b|
167|de10cc|    /// Normalizes UI-provided line indices.
168|2cbc84|    ///
169|20e2d8|    /// The editor UI typically uses 0-based indices for line iteration. We clamp
170|6014a1|    /// to a minimum of 0 to avoid negative values.
171|b22942|    private func canonicalLine(_ line: Int) -> Int {
172|20f91b|        max(0, line)
173|27e597|    }

175|5ce9fa|    func hasBreakpoint(file: String, line: Int) -> Bool {
176|345f2b|        let fileId = canonicalFileId(file)
177|e74a32|        let line = canonicalLine(line)
178|c135e6|        return breakpointsByFile[fileId]?.contains(line) == true
179|27e597|    }
180|adc83b|
181|c99ea4|    func toggleBreakpoint(file: String, line: Int) {
182|345f2b|        let fileId = canonicalFileId(file)
183|e74a32|        let line = canonicalLine(line)
184|adc83b|
185|5c5f53|        // IMPORTANT: mutate via a copy so @Published emits reliably for collection changes.
186|8dfb09|        var dict = breakpointsByFile
187|2eb6b8|        var set = dict[fileId] ?? []
188|adc83b|
189|e49052|        if set.contains(line) {
190|646b56|            set.remove(line)
191|b31999|        } else {
192|ec8126|            set.insert(line)
193|5f3077|        }
194|adc83b|
195|be2c1c|        if set.isEmpty {
196|9e6e9b|            dict.removeValue(forKey: fileId)
197|b31999|        } else {
198|63e6d5|            dict[fileId] = set
199|5f3077|        }
200|adc83b|
201|718dd5|        breakpointsByFile = dict
202|27e597|    }
203|adc83b|
204|1f1804|    func setBreakpoint(file: String, line: Int, isEnabled: Bool) {
205|7614bc|        // UI-only model currently treats "enabled" as "present/absent".
206|de12f2|        // (Real debugger integration can extend this to store disabled breakpoints.)
207|771692|        if isEnabled {
208|e95a4e|            if !hasBreakpoint(file: file, line: line) {
209|b3cdcc|                toggleBreakpoint(file: file, line: line)
210|a7dc16|            }
211|b31999|        } else {
212|d0d375|            removeBreakpoint(file: file, line: line)
213|5f3077|        }
214|27e597|    }

216|de9666|    func removeBreakpoint(file: String, line: Int) {

623|cb0d35|                try Self.runWithProcess(task: task, workspaceRootURL: self.workspaceRootURL) { chunk in
624|3d4547|                    Task { @MainActor in
625|6d7bc4|                        TaskOutputPanelManager.shared.append(chunk, to: .tasks)
626|c9717a|                    }
627|4e2d32|                }
628|adc83b|
629|ed8fb4|                let elapsed = Date().timeIntervalSince(start)
630|df2890|                Task { @MainActor in
631|ebe60b|                    TaskOutputPanelManager.shared.appendLine(String(format: "[Task] Finished (%.2fs)", elapsed), to: .tasks)
632|d34780|                    self.isRunning = false
633|01f0a7|                    self.runningTaskLabel = nil
634|4e2d32|                }
635|91b9a2|            } catch {
636|df2890|                Task { @MainActor in
637|0d776b|                    TaskOutputPanelManager.shared.appendLine("[Task] Error: \(error.localizedDescription)", to: .tasks)
638|c862fb|                    self.lastErrorMessage = error.localizedDescription
639|d34780|                    self.isRunning = false
640|01f0a7|                    self.runningTaskLabel = nil
641|4e2d32|                }
642|a7dc16|            }
643|5f3077|        }
644|27e597|    }
645|adc83b|
646|bee245|    private static func runWithProcess(
647|e5dc05|        task: VSCodeTask,
648|82b696|        workspaceRootURL: URL?,
649|4bc83d|        onOutput: @escaping (String) -> Void
650|53fcb2|    ) throws {
651|f2b054|#if os(macOS)
652|6d92f9|        let process = Process()
653|adc83b|
654|954421|        if let cwd = workspaceRootURL {
655|9f27f7|            process.currentDirectoryURL = cwd
656|5f3077|        }
657|adc83b|
658|cb7289|        let expandedCommand = expandVariables(task.command, workspaceRootURL: workspaceRootURL)
659|18c5c4|        let expandedArgs = (task.args ?? []).map { expandVariables($0, workspaceRootURL: workspaceRootURL) }
660|adc83b|
661|01b605|        switch task.type {
662|25e00e|        case .shell:
663|e6c111|            // Use a login shell so things like `swift`/`npm` resolve from PATH (where supported).
664|a1da9c|            // Note: This is expected to work on macOS / Mac Catalyst. On iPadOS, spawning processes
665|10d484|            // may be restricted; errors will be reported to the output panel.
666|c56cfe|            process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/bin/zsh")
667|11ebc0|            let commandLine = ([expandedCommand] + expandedArgs)
668|6598dc|                .map(shellEscape)
669|9739e2|                .joined(separator: " ")
670|9b4d66|            process.arguments = ["-lc", commandLine]
671|adc83b|
672|0cfd10|        case .process:
673|728cfa|            // Use /usr/bin/env so a bare command name can be resolved via PATH.
674|9dce62|            process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/env")
675|a102d5|            process.arguments = [expandedCommand] + expandedArgs
676|5f3077|        }
677|adc83b|
678|9cbcc0|        let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
679|edd8ac|        let stderrPipe = Pipe()
680|62a0a1|        process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
681|7dc19f|        process.standardError = stderrPipe
682|adc83b|
683|059b19|        let lock = NSLock()
684|f7e808|        func forward(_ data: Data) {
685|52e34c|            guard !data.isEmpty else { return }
686|3d8279|            if let s = String(data: data, encoding: .utf8), !s.isEmpty {
687|1a0efa|                lock.lock()
688|ca3df0|                onOutput(s)
689|369d2c|                lock.unlock()
690|a7dc16|            }
691|5f3077|        }
692|adc83b|
693|1e04df|        stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readabilityHandler = { handle in
694|4eeee5|            forward(handle.availableData)
695|5f3077|        }
696|86c33c|        stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readabilityHandler = { handle in
697|4eeee5|            forward(handle.availableData)
698|5f3077|        }
699|adc83b|
700|949e5a|        try process.run()
701|143813|        process.waitUntilExit()
702|adc83b|
703|f6d30d|        stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readabilityHandler = nil
704|de4647|        stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readabilityHandler = nil
705|adc83b|
706|1a961c|        // Flush any remaining data.
707|78de64|        forward(stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile())
708|99b3d6|        forward(stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile())
709|adc83b|
710|fe411a|        if process.terminationStatus != 0 {
711|a632fc|            throw NSError(
712|489020|                domain: "TasksManager",
713|cad6d3|                code: Int(process.terminationStatus),
714|701bc2|                userInfo: [NSLocalizedDescriptionKey: "Task exited with code \(process.terminationStatus)"]
715|43d041|            )
716|5f3077|        }
717|97d907|#else
718|3af01f|        // Process execution not available on iOS
719|59a7d5|        onOutput("Error: Task execution is not available on iOS\n")
720|b2fbe2|        throw NSError(
721|78e5e5|            domain: "TasksManager",
722|bf3b57|            code: 1,
723|a20e53|            userInfo: [NSLocalizedDescriptionKey: "Task execution is not available on iOS"]
724|3143a4|        )
725|3f6acf|#endif
726|27e597|    }
727|adc83b|
728|ae92ad|    // MARK: - JSONC helpers
729|adc83b|
730|a26719|    /// VS Code `tasks.json` often uses JSON with comments (JSONC). This strips
731|11a55b|    /// both `//` line comments and `/* ... */` block comments.
732|fb989d|    private static func stripJSONComments(_ input: String) -> String {
733|5749dc|        let blockPattern = "/\\*[^*]*\\*+(?:[^/*][^*]*\\*+)*/"
734|e0e74b|        let linePattern = "(?m)//.*$"
735|adc83b|
736|aec1b9|        let withoutBlocks = input.replacingOccurrences(of: blockPattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
737|1e4b82|        let withoutLines = withoutBlocks.replacingOccurrences(of: linePattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
738|2c31a3|        return withoutLines
739|27e597|    }
740|adc83b|
741|2bbb9c|    // MARK: - Variable expansion
742|adc83b|
743|2af0bf|    private static func expandVariables(_ value: String, workspaceRootURL: URL?) -> String {
744|7c78bd|        var out = value
745|69ca93|        if let workspaceRootURL {
746|059e23|            out = out.replacingOccurrences(of: "${workspaceFolder}", with: workspaceRootURL.path)
747|5f3077|        }
748|300c03|        // `${file}` is not currently resolved (needs active editor tab), but we keep it intact.
749|9231ab|        return out
750|27e597|    }
751|adc83b|
752|cffd9d|    private static func shellEscape(_ s: String) -> String {
753|6b5897|        if s.isEmpty { return "''" }
754|68194e|        // Basic single-quote escaping for zsh/bash.
755|314dc1|        if s.contains(where: { $0.isWhitespace || $0 == "\"" || $0 == "'" || $0 == "\\" || $0 == "(" || $0 == ")" }) {
756|09f4bd|            return "'" + s.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "'\\''") + "'"
757|5f3077|        }
758|48af33|        return s
759|27e597|    }

149|288471|        lastErrorMessage = nil
150|adc83b|
151|86eb27|        guard let workspaceRootURL else {
152|9f6110|            // No workspace: keep templates.
153|671444|            if configs.isEmpty {
154|116dea|                configs = LaunchConfig.builtInTemplates

162|3556d1|            .appendingPathComponent("launch.json", isDirectory: false)

248|e91279|        // Remove block comments first.

224|049941|    // MARK: - Private Methods
225|b4687f|    
226|886d26|    /// Sets up the Combine pipeline with debounce and throttle operators.
227|7cfeb1|    /// 
228|2302ea|    /// Pipeline flow:
229|fcd00b|    /// 1. typingSubject receives events
230|a7ce76|    /// 2. debounce(0.3s): Wait 300ms after user stops typing
231|a5971a|    /// 3. throttle(2.0s): Max 1 event per 2 seconds (latest=true for responsive updates)
232|c17292|    /// 4. removeDuplicates: Filter identical events
233|627455|    /// 5. filter: Remove empty/unworthy contexts
234|6f85e6|    /// 6. flatMap: Execute async fetch with cancellation support
235|2181d5|    private func setupSuggestionPipeline() {
236|ca13c2|        pipelineCancellable = typingSubject
237|0245e4|            // STEP 1: DEBOUNCE (300ms)
238|70cff9|            // Wait 300ms after user stops typing before processing
239|d9fce5|            // This prevents firing requests while user is actively typing
240|84dd17|            .debounce(for: .seconds(debounceInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main)
241|3070d1|            
242|89fc5a|            // STEP 2: THROTTLE (2 seconds)
243|dbb01b|            // Maximum 1 request per 2 seconds
244|bce2c6|            // latest=true ensures we get the most recent event if multiple occur within throttle window
245|ecc467|            .throttle(for: .seconds(throttleInterval), scheduler: DispatchQueue.main, latest: true)
246|3070d1|            
247|844254|            // STEP 3: REMOVE DUPLICATES
248|413909|            // Filter out events with identical content and position
249|0a99da|            // This prevents duplicate API calls for the same context
250|cf49b3|            .removeDuplicates()
251|3070d1|            
252|202ed6|            // STEP 4: FILTER WORTHY CONTEXTS
253|a23af6|            // Only proceed if we have meaningful content to get suggestions for
254|845b1e|            .filter { [weak self] event in
255|06905f|                guard let self = self else { return false }
256|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
257|cc659b|                return self.shouldRequestSuggestion(context: context)
258|a7dc16|            }
259|3070d1|            
260|339920|            // STEP 5: FLATMAP TO ASYNC FETCH
261|2bc815|            // Transform each event into a publisher that fetches suggestions
262|dbc22b|            // This creates a new async context that can be cancelled
263|11fcbf|            .flatMap { [weak self] event -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> in
264|ec615d|                guard let self = self else {
265|6156c3|                    return Just(nil).eraseToAnyPublisher()
266|4e2d32|                }
267|216278|                
268|531968|                let context = self.extractContext(from: event.content, at: event.position)
269|6830af|                return self.createFetchPublisher(for: context)
270|a7dc16|            }
271|4de6c5|            // Ensure we receive on main thread for UI updates
272|a8597a|            .receive(on: DispatchQueue.main)
273|1051e2|            .sink { [weak self] suggestion in
274|518c9e|                self?.currentSuggestion = suggestion
275|02c979|                self?.isLoading = false
276|a7dc16|            }
277|27e597|    }
278|b4687f|    
279|984754|    /// Creates a Combine publisher that performs the async suggestion fetch.
280|f2b66e|    /// This allows the fetch to be cancelled when new events arrive.
281|4c0331|    private func createFetchPublisher(for context: SuggestionContext) -> AnyPublisher<String?, Never> {
282|c401a0|        // Cancel any existing fetch task
283|f12123|        fetchTask?.cancel()
284|d6ed84|        
285|1c5d21|        // Create new async task for fetching
286|6b1f07|        let task = Task { [weak self] () -> String? in
287|8c11f0|            guard let self = self else { return nil }
288|3070d1|            
289|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
290|7494b5|                self.isLoading = true
291|db594a|                self.lastError = nil

303|15034a|                return nil

322|27e597|    }

320|b8b714|    func sendMessage(_ content: String, context: String? = nil) async {
321|915e6f|        guard hasValidAPIKey() else {
322|06856b|            error = "Please set your API key in settings"
323|bef5d6|            return
324|5f3077|        }
325|d6ed84|        
326|e352e6|        let userMessage = ChatMessage(role: .user, content: content)
327|382c05|        currentSession.messages.append(userMessage)
328|aa2963|        updateSession()
329|d6ed84|        
330|8495c1|        // Update title if first message
331|8926e1|        if currentSession.messages.count == 1 {
332|066ce6|            currentSession.title = String(content.prefix(50))
333|e749a7|            updateSession()
334|5f3077|        }
335|d6ed84|        
336|d52924|        isLoading = true
337|0406ba|        error = nil
338|dc34fb|        streamingResponse = ""
339|d6ed84|        
340|4da690|        do {
341|ce5098|            let response = try await makeAPIRequest(messages: currentSession.messages, context: context)
342|70672e|            let assistantMessage = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response, codeBlocks: extractCodeBlocks(from: response))
343|c17117|            currentSession.messages.append(assistantMessage)
344|e749a7|            updateSession()
345|853889|        } catch {
346|97a9c5|            self.error = error.localizedDescription
347|5f3077|        }
348|d6ed84|        
349|295f36|        isLoading = false
350|27e597|    }

388|90c566|    private func sendAndGetResponse(_ prompt: String) async -> String {

392|d6ed84|

394|0406ba|        error = nil
395|d6ed84|        
396|4da690|        do {
397|3b5c4f|            let messages = [ChatMessage(role: .user, content: prompt)]
398|153d92|            let response = try await makeAPIRequest(messages: messages, context: nil)
399|612c3f|            isLoading = false
400|d392d0|            return response
